The connection manager bases further\\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n37:  */\\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n40:   Continue,\\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\\n42:   //\\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n45:   //\\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n49:   StopIteration,\\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\\n52:   //\\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\\n56:   //\\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. This causes ASSERTs in\\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\\n83:   //\\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. ContinueDecoding() MUST\\n89:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n90:   //\\n91:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\\n92:   // iteration to resume.\\n93:   //\\n94:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\\n95:   // be sent to the user. (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto) defines the configuration schema. The http_filters field (line 471) contains a repeated list of HttpFilter messages (defined at line 1339). FilterChainHelper.processFilters() iterates through each filter configuration and creates FilterFactoryCallbacks by invoking the registered filter factory. This creates a FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl instance (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 913), which is passed to the filter factory callback.\\n\\n## Filter Installation\\nThe filter factory callback uses FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface methods (envoy/http/filter.h, line 1224) to add filters:\\n- addStreamDecoderFilter() - adds decoder-only filters\\n- addStreamEncoderFilter() - adds encoder-only filters  \\n- addStreamFilter() - adds bidirectional filters\\n- addAccessLogHandler() - registers access log handlers\\n\\nFilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps these calls to add filters to the FilterManager's decoder and encoder filter lists (lines 918-938), wrapping them in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter for state tracking.\\n\\n## Key Integration Points\\n1. ConnectionManagerImpl (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h) creates HTTP streams and manages the overall connection\\n2. DownstreamFilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 1094) specializes FilterManager with downstream-specific behavior like local reply handling\\n3. This creates a FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl instance (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 913), which is passed to the filter factory callback.\\n\\n## Filter Installation\\nThe filter factory callback uses FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface methods (envoy/http/filter.h, line 1224) to add filters:\\n- addStreamDecoderFilter() - adds decoder-only filters\\n- addStreamEncoderFilter() - adds encoder-only filters  \\n- addStreamFilter() - adds bidirectional filters\\n- addAccessLogHandler() - registers access log handlers\\n\\nFilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps these calls to add filters to the FilterManager's decoder and encoder filter lists (lines 918-938), wrapping them in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter for state tracking.\\n\\n## Key Integration Points\\n1. ConnectionManagerImpl (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h) creates HTTP streams and manages the overall connection\\n2. DownstreamFilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 1094) specializes FilterManager with downstream-specific behavior like local reply handling\\n3. The filter factory pattern allows plugins to register and provide filter implementations that are dynamically instantiated at stream creation time\\n4. The FilterChainHelper template supports both static filter configuration and dynamic configuration discovery via ECDS\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
